***давать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> (162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dāvàti</i>. Composed as if from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">davátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give</li>
<li>to let, to allow</li>
<li>to hit, to strike, to clip</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put out, to consent to sex</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>дава́ться</a> (4619)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>дава́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">davátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:даться.html>да́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let oneself, to allow oneself (to be caught, to be cheated, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>дава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обида.html>оби́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>davátʹsja</b> v obídu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not to allow oneself to be pushed around/over</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come easily
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:даваться.html>дава́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:иностранный.html>иностра́нные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языки́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú ne <b>daválisʹ</b> inostránnyje jazykí.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Foreign languages didn't come easily to him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***давить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a> (4345)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dāvìti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">davítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to weigh, to lie heavy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>да́вит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́шу</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sneg <b>dávit</b> na krýšu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the snow weighs on the roof</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to crush</li>
<li>to press, to squeeze
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ягода.html>я́годы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>davítʹ</b> jágody</i> ― <span class="e-translation">press the juice out of berries</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лимон.html>лимо́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>davítʹ</b> limón</i> ― <span class="e-translation">squeeze a lemon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:виноград.html>виногра́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>davítʹ</b> vinográd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tramp grapes</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to suppress, to stifle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kill, to destroy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put pressure on, to pressurize, to pressure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>да́вят</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выступить.html>вы́ступил</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заявление.html>заявле́нием</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na nevó <b>dávjat</b>, štóby on výstupil s zajavlénijem</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he is being pressurized/pressured to make a statement</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>daví</b> na menjá!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">don't get hard on me!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давиться.html>дави́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">davítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавиться.html>подави́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to choke <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">be unable to breathe because of obstruction of the windpipe</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давка.html>да́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dávka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давка.html>да́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давка.html>да́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давка.html>да́вок</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давление.html>давле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">davlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давление.html>давле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давление.html>давле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давление.html>давле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pressure (physics: amount of force divided by area)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:давность.html>да́вность</a> (9442)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давний.html>да́вний</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dávnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давность.html>да́вность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dávnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давность.html>да́вности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давность.html>да́вности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давность.html>да́вностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>remoteness (in time), antiquity; long standing; time limitation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:давность.html>да́вность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обычай.html>обы́чая</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dávnostʹ</b> étovo obýčaja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the antiquity of this custom</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:давность.html>да́вность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:событие.html>собы́тий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dávnostʹ</b> sobýtij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">remoteness of events</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">десятиле́тняя <b><a href = vnd.unilang:давность.html>да́вность</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">desjatilétnjaja <b>dávnostʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">ten years' prescription</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>срок</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:давность.html>да́вности</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">srok <b>dávnosti</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">statute of limitation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> (64)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dáže</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>even
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dáže</b> i</i> ― <span class="e-translation">even</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dáže</b> ne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not even</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жете</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>заме́длить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:остановить.html>останови́ть</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Móžete zamédlitʹ íli <b>dáže</b> ostanovítʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You can slow down or <b>even</b> stop.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***далеко.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:далеко.html>далеко́</a> (549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:далеко.html>далеко́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dalekó</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-далеко́" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)да́льше</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>far, far off, far away</li>
<li>a long way</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">далёкий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">daljókij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дальневосточный.html>дальневосто́чный</a> (17051)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальний.html>да́льний</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dálʹnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восток.html>восто́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vostók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальний.html>да́льний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:восток.html>восто́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Dálʹnij Vostók</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Far East</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дальнейший.html>дальне́йший</a> (1512)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальнейший.html>дальне́йший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dalʹnéjšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дальний.html>да́льний</a> (1322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальний.html>да́льний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dálʹnij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:далее.html>да́лее</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:даль.html>да́лей</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)да́льше</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальнейший.html>дальне́йший</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дальний.html>да́льний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>far, distant</li>
<li>remote</li>
<li>long</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="профессиональное">проф.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:имеющий.html>име́ющий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:длительный.html>дли́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>срок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствия</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ценный.html>це́нных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́гах</a>) <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальнобойный.html>дальнобо́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dalʹnobójnyj</span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> long-range <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of weapons, munitions, weapon fire</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

***дальновидный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дальновидный.html>дальнови́дный</a> (24396)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальний.html>да́льний</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dálʹnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vid</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальновидный.html>дальнови́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dalʹnovídnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дальнови́днее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дальнови́дней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>far-sighted, forward-looking, prudent</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальний.html>да́льний</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dálʹnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальность.html>да́льность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dálʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальность.html>да́льности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальность.html>да́льности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дальность.html>да́льностей</a></b>)
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">dame</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">domina</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lady</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">domus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dṓm</i>, from root <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dem-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to build</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дама.html>да́ма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dáma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дама.html>да́мы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дама.html>да́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́м</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дама.html>да́ма</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dáma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дамский.html>да́мский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dámskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lady's, ladies'
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дамский.html>да́мский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:портной.html>портно́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dámskij</b> portnój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ladies' tailor</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дамский.html>да́мский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парикмахер.html>парикма́хер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dámskij</b> parikmáxer</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hairdresser</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дамский.html>да́мская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мната</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dámskaja</b> kómnata</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ladies' room</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***дань.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дань.html>дань</a> (9991)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*danь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дань.html>дань</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">danʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дань.html>да́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дань.html>да́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дань.html>да́ней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>contribution, tribute</li>
<li>tributary</li>
<li>homage, tribute
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдавать.html>отдава́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дань.html>дань</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уважение.html>уваже́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otdavátʹ <b>danʹ</b> uvažénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pay homage to</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>toll

***дар.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дар.html>дар</a> (2362)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">даръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">darŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*darъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gift</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*déh₃rom</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дар.html>дар</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dar</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дар.html>да́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дар.html>дары́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дар.html>даро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gift, present</li>
<li>talent, aptitude</li></ol>
